1.5(1): gsas mkhar rin po che spyi spungs kyi nang nas/ gsal byed mngon 
1.6(1): shes rtags kyi sgrub pa zhal phye nas/ zhi khro sprul pa'i tshogs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /
1.7(1): 7 'di ni mun sel sgron ma ste/ bsnyen bsgrub dbang dang bcas pa yi/ gtsang 
1.8(1): ma ldan pa'i gshen rab kyis/ 'das dang ma 'ongs da lta yi/ sngon dang skad cig phyi 
1.9(1): ma las/ don dam kun rdzob bden pa yi/ blo dang blo las 'das pa yi/ bye brag so 
1.10(1): so'i ye shes kyis/ blo 'das me long 'od gsal ba'i/ dngos por 'das pa gnyis 
1.11(1): med mnyam/ mnyam pas bya ba'i 'bad rtsol bral/ bral bas mtshan med stong pa 
1.12(1): nyid/ don dam bde chen kun bzang ngang / ci yang ma yin cir gsal ba/ gnyis 
1.13(1): med ka dag byang chub sems/ mkha' la sprin med 'od gsal bzhin/ rnam dag dri 
1.14(1): med ye sangs rgyas/ de don gsal la dmigs med na/ don dam dngos po mthong 
1.15(1): ba ste/ mkha' la nyi ma shar ba 'dra/ sems ni nam mkha' ye dag la/ cho 'phrul 
1.16(1): rtog pa'i rgyu rkyen gyis/ dngos po kun bzang don dang bral/ rgyu rkyen las kyi gzed 
2.1(1): bshams nas/ 'khor ba'i gnas su ltung sbyor byed/ bye brag rgyu rkyen 'phen shugs 
2.2(1): kyis/ sdong po yal ga lo 'dab bzhin/ 'khor bas 'khor ba'i skye 'phen byas/ kun 
2.3(1): rdzob 'khor bas rags rgyas las/ rnam byang don dam lam la 'grib/ spyi ru de ltar 
2.4(1): sde gcig kyang / bye brag rigs drug sems can rnams/ rgyu rkyen ngan pas 'bras bu 
2.5(1): ni/ tshe lus bsod nams so sor bskal/ khyad par mi rnams las dbang gis/ brgya 
2.6(1): dang bcu drug zhen rtas pas/ 'khor ba'i gnas su kha brgyud pa/ don gyi shes par 
2.7(1): mngon mthong nas/ skye dang rgas dang na dang 'chi/ 'khor ba'i gnas su sbyor mthong 
2.8(1): na/ log pa mngon du shes pa yin/ de bzhin mtho ris kun gyis kyang / 'khor ba 
2.9(1): ya ngar don shes la/ thabs dang shes rab don 'brel cing / skyed pa'i rgyu la len 
2.10(1): pa yis/ ye shes bskyed pa'i sa bon spros/ mkha' la rgyan tshogs thim pa bzhin/ ba 
2.11(1): ga'i klong nas 'od rdzogs nas/ kun bzang bde ba'i ngang nyid du/ lhang nge lhan ne 
2.12(1): mnyam bzhag pas/ rang rig khong nas shar ba yis/ rgyun chad med pa'i rtogs pa 
2.13(1): ru/ khams gsum thugs la yongs rdzogs nas/ don la mngon shes shar ba yis/ pra 
2.14(1): rtags rab tu bstan pa yin/

2.17(1): yis nyams sod 'byung / nam mkha'i dbyings su 'phur ba dang / nyi zla rta ru zhon pa 
2.18(1): dang / gza' skar tshogs por 'phen pa dang / lho sprin gos su gyon pa dang / gza' 
2.19(1): chen thod du bcing pa dang / rgu tshigs shul la 'grim pa dang / gzha' tshon thag pa

3.1(1): rang gis shes pa dang / bya rgyal khyung la zhon pa dang / bar snang khams su lding ba 
3.2(1): dang / ba dan ru mtshon phyar ba dang / smrigs kyi thag pas 'dren pa dang / gzugs

4.1(1): 'gyil dang / dgra ma zun du rdzu 'phrul ston/ lus la mtshon zug phyam du lhung / me

5.4(1): dang / gcan zan bya dang ban glang nya/ sbal pa'i phyi ba khyu gu gser/ klu gnyan sa

5.17(1): ltung / lha dang yig 'bru gsal gnas na/ 'gro bzang lha mi'i lhum du zhugs/ yum gyi

6.7(1): zhan/ 'gal dang mthun pa de bzhin shes/ chu ni tsha grang khol bur gzer/ grang dang
